# Generic Magic Apparel


**See Also**:

- [Magic Items](Skyrim_Magic_Items.md): General information on magic items and how they appear.
- [Armor](Skyrim_Armor.md): All of the basic (unenchanted) armor in the game.
- [Clothing](Skyrim_Clothing.md): All of the basic (unenchanted) clothing and jewelry in the game.
- [Leveled Items](Skyrim_Leveled_Items.md): Leveled magic apparel, generally received as quest rewards.
- [Unique Items](Skyrim_Unique_Items.md): Unique apparel, available from merchants or received as quest rewards.
- [Artifacts](Skyrim_Artifacts.md): Unusually powerful one-of-a-kind apparel.

[Tempering](Skyrim_Workbench.md) any magic armor requires the [Arcane Blacksmith](Skyrim_Arcane_Blacksmith.md) perk to be unlocked. The type of ingot (or other material) necessary for the upgrade, as well as which [Smithing](Skyrim_Smithing.md) perk augments the upgrade, is the same as for the base version of the armor. The base version of each armor is highlighted via a link in the armor name; that link leads to the page detailing the base armor. Clothing can not be upgraded.

Unless noted otherwise, all of these items can be disenchanted.

The levels in the table describe the *base* level at which an item begins to show up randomly for the player, and appears to only be a hard minimum level for shops. Lower level items will also randomly appear, but so will higher level armors in certain "loot" situations: potentially up to at least 12 levels "early".

The Dragonplate Helmet (d7a74) and Daedric Helmet (d7ae6) of Extreme Magicka are, in fact, Peerless. They are mislabeled as Extreme in-game.

## [Fortify Stamina](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Stamina)
Note: There are no chest pieces in this category. Although some fortify stamina items are named "Orcish Armor of..." or "Steel Armor of...", these items are actually boots.
